## Legend & UI Components

### Status Indicators
- ğŸŸ¢ **Green Circle** - Approved, Active, On Track, Completed
- ğŸŸ¡ **Yellow Circle** - Pending, In Progress, At Risk
- ğŸ”´ **Red Circle** - Rejected, Overdue, Off Track
- âšª **White Circle** - Draft, Not Started
- âœ… **Check Mark** - Completed, Approved
- âŒ **X Mark** - Rejected, Cancelled
- âš ï¸  **Warning** - Alert, Attention Required

### Common UI Elements
- **[Button]** - Clickable action button
- **[Dropdown â–¼]** - Dropdown select menu
- **[â˜‘ï¸]** - Checkbox (selected)
- **[â˜]** - Checkbox (unselected)
- **(â€¢)** - Radio button (selected)
- **( )** - Radio button (unselected)
- **[âœ• Close]** - Close modal/dialog
- **â–ˆâ–ˆâ–ˆâ–ˆâ–ˆâ–ˆâ–ˆâ–ˆâ–‘â–‘** - Progress bar
- **ğŸ“…** - Date picker icon
- **ğŸ”** - Search icon
- **ğŸ“** - Attachment icon

### Typography
- **Bold Text** - Headers, labels, important information
- *Italic Text* - Supplementary information, notes
- `Monospace` - Code, IDs, technical values
- â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€ - Section dividers
- â•”â•â•â•â•— - Table borders

## Navigation Flow

### Leave Management Flow
```
My Leave Dashboard â†’ Request New Leave â†’ Save Draft / Submit
                  â†“
            Leave Approvals â†’ Approve / Reject â†’ Email Notification
                  â†“
            Updated Leave Status â†’ Employee Notified
```

### Timesheet Flow
```
Timesheet Dashboard â†’ Weekly Entry Grid â†’ Save Draft / Submit
                   â†“
            Approval Dashboard â†’ Approve / Reject â†’ Payroll Integration
                   â†“
            Approved Timesheet â†’ Employee Notified
```

### Expense Flow
```
Expense Dashboard â†’ Submit Expense â†’ Upload Receipt â†’ Submit
                 â†“
            Approval Dashboard â†’ Approve / Reject â†’ Reimbursement
                 â†“
            Payment Processing â†’ Employee Paid
```

### Invoice Flow
```
Invoice Dashboard â†’ Create Invoice â†’ Add Line Items â†’ Send
                 â†“
            Client Receives â†’ Payment Received â†’ Record Payment
                 â†“
            Invoice Marked Paid
```

### Performance Flow
```
Performance Dashboard â†’ Self-Assessment â†’ Submit
                     â†“
            Manager Review â†’ Rate & Comment â†’ Submit
                     â†“
            Employee Notified â†’ View Review â†’ Set New Goals
```

---

## Mobile Responsive Views

All screens are fully responsive and adapt to mobile viewports:
- **Desktop (>1024px)**: Full sidebar + main content
- **Tablet (768-1024px)**: Collapsible sidebar
- **Mobile (<768px)**: Hidden sidebar with hamburger menu, stacked layouts

---

## Accessibility Features

- **Keyboard Navigation**: All interactive elements keyboard-accessible
- **Screen Reader Support**: ARIA labels on all components
- **High Contrast**: Status colors meet WCAG AA standards
- **Focus Indicators**: Clear focus states on all buttons/inputs
- **Responsive Text**: Minimum 14px font size, scalable
